1: const http = require('http');
2: 
3: function fetchUrl(url) {
4:   return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
5:     http.get(url, (res) => {
6:       let data = '';
7:       res.on('data', (chunk) => { data += chunk; });
8:       res.on('end', () => { resolve(data); });
9:     }).on('error', reject);
10:   });
11: }
12: 
13: async function run() {
14:   try {
15:     console.log('Fetching supabase.js from local server...');
16:     const supabaseJs = await fetchUrl('http://localhost:3000/supabase.js');

  async function getUserType() {
    const session = await getSession();
    if (!session || !session.user) return null;

    const profile = await getProfile(session.user.id);
    if (profile) return profile.user_type;

    // Fallback to metadata
    return session.user.user_metadata?.user_type || 'student';
  }
